==⚠  Switch to EXCALIDRAW VIEW in the MORE OPTIONS menu of this document. ⚠==


# Text Elements
[ ] LastInstalled
    Datetime of the last update installed on the system
[ ] LastUpdate
    Datetime of the last time evaluated ^W91QE12k

[ ] (XXXXX) - five digit Dell identifier, driver description, datetime ^ZWULNiX2

[ ] ExecutionComplete
    True/False
[ ] ReturnCode
    Int of the last return code from dcu-cli.exe ^0MhUnLfi
